## Library: IMMZD2DTPolioBOPVPlusIPVLogic 

| | |
| :--- | :--- |
| *Official URL*:http://smart.who.int/immunizations/Library/IMMZD2DTPolioBOPVPlusIPVLogic | *Version*:0.2.0 |
| Draft as of 2026-03-31 | *Computable Name*:IMMZD2DTPolioBOPVPlusIPVLogic |

 
This library defines decision support logic for the IMMZ.D2.DT.Polio.bOPV plus IPV decision table in the Immunization CPG
